 Mahashivaratri is considered to be the biggest and auspicious day of Shiva worship
 is shiv mandiron main bhakton kaa baari jamaavada dekha ja saktaa he
 Among all the Devas, Shiva is the only God who becomes very happy with the devotion and worship of his devotees
 is baar 24 farvari ko mahashivaratri manaai jaaegi
 Let us know about the auspicious time of worship on the day of Maha Shivaratri
 
 
 mahashivaratri hinduon ke bade tyohaar or vraton main se ek mana gaya he
 It is believed that at the beginning of creation, on this day, midnight Lord Shankar was descended from Brahma as Rudra
 pralay kii vela main isi din pradosh ke samay bhagwaan shiv tandav karte hue brahmad ko tisare netra kii jwaala se samaapt kar dete hai
 That is why it is called Maha Shivaratri
 jaane, koun sa phool chadhaane se shiv ji hote hai prasann
 
 
 Apart from this, in many places in India, it is also believed that Lord Shiva was married on this day
 vaise to har maheene masik shivaratri manaai jaati he lekin phalgun ke maheene kii shivaratri ko hi mahashivaratri kehete hai
 Mahashivaratri is celebrated for two days, so Mahashivratri is falling on 24th February, but due to the fall of Trayodashi, Mahashivaratri will be worshiped on 25th February
 25 farvari ko shanivaar ko chaturdashi tithi raat 9:20 tak rahegi
 Due to this, Mahashivaratri can be worshiped from the night of 24 to 25 February
 rudrabhishek se prasann hote hai shiv ji, har manokamana kar denge puripuja or muhoort kaa samaynishith kaal puja- 24:08 se 24:59paaran kaa samay- 06:54 se 15:24 (25 farvari)chaturdashi tithi aarambh- 21:38 (24 farvari)chaturdashi tithi samaapt- 21:20 (25 farvari)ghar main he mandir to rakhen 9 in baton kaa khaas dhyaan This suicide point is 16 km from Muzaffarnagar

 yah puche jane par ki kya dilli ‘balaatkaar kii rajdhani’ banati ja rahi he, unhone kaha ki aisa nahin he
 He declined to discuss the incidents of rape overall
 unhone kaha, ‘‘ham is ghatana par charchaa karte hai
 If we discuss this in totality, i will say something that is politically incorrect 
 aap use galat dhang se pesh karenge
 In response to a question, he said that the victims' mobile phones were not used at the time of the incident
 sutron ne bataaya ki police bas ke sisitivi footage praapt karne main safal rahi jisaki madad se bas kii pahchaan sambhav ho saki
 Investigators sent SMS to the victims' mobile phones to trace the accused, which was snatched away by the attackers
 tippaniyan The anger of the people erupted over this incident
 jawahar laal nehru vishvavidhyalay ke chaatro ne vasantkunj police thane ke baahar pradarshan kiya

 sarkaar or police ko yah sunishchit karnaa chahie ki dilli main mahilaon kaa utpeedan ruke
 Simply installing CCTV will not do
 ’’ Doctors said that the condition of the victim student still remains critical but 'better than yesterday'
 dilli police ayukta niraj kumaar ne kaha ki chartered bas ke chaalak, uske bhai or do logon ko giraftaar kar liya gaya he jabaki baaki do aropiyon kii dharpakad ke liye bade paimaane par abhiyaan shuru kiya gaya he
 The chartered bus was not legally permitted to run on the normal route
